         <div class="special-numbering" id="slide-title">
          105 Awesome but Affordable Gifts For Men
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="body-wrap">
         <div class="slide-body" id="slide-body">
          <p>
           Stumped about what to give the men in your life? Look no further than this gift guide that's chock-full of affordable and
           <a class="sugar-inline-link" href="http://www.popsugar.com/DIY" target="_blank" title="Latest photos and news for DIY">
            DIY
           </a>
           gifts for men of all ages. These gifts would make awesome presents for everyone in your life. Click on to get started on your gift shopping!
          </p>
          <p>
           And when you're done shopping for him, here's a list of
           <a href="http://www.savvysugar.com/Cheap-Christmas-Gifts-Women-32491647">
            affordable presents for women
           </a>
           .
          </p>

            <div class="body">
             <span class="comment-body">
              <p>
               LOL. True. My tips for an affordable Christmas -
              </p>
              <p>
               1) Shop online. Walmart, Amazon, etc. has everything you could possibly want with free shipping.  Plus, you get to avoid holiday traffic.
              </p>
              <p>
               2) Use coupon sites like retail me not.
              </p>
              <p>
               3) Give gift cards or cash. Most physical gifts will go unused.
              </p>
              <p>
               4) Cut back spending in other parts of your life.  Dont limit it to just Christmas.  Examples - $20/month cell phone from Tmobile, $24/month car insurance from Insurance Panda, $15/month gym from Planet Fitness.
              </p>
              <p>
               5) Re-Gift old presents that you never used. Dont just throw them away!
              </p>
             </span>
            </div>

              <p>
               How to save money at Christmas -
              </p>
              <p>
               1) Shop online. Walmart, Amazon, etc. has everything you could possibly want with free shipping.  Plus, you get to avoid holiday traffic.
              </p>
              <p>
               2) Use coupon sites like retail me not.
              </p>
              <p>
               3) Give gift cards or cash. Most physical gifts will go unused.
              </p>
              <p>
               4) Cut back spending in other parts of your life.  Dont limit it to just Christmas.  Examples - $20/month cell phone from Tmobile, $24/month car insurance from 4AutoInsuranceQuote, $15/month gym from Planet Fitness.
              </p>
              <p>
               5) Re-Gift old presents that you never used. Dont just throw them away!
              </p>

             <span class="comment-body">
              <p>
               Why is this labeled "for men?" These are not gifts "for men." This is a pish-posh combination of gifts good for cyclists, guitar/bass players, tea-drinkers, Star-Trek fans, booze-drinkers, and people who just like mustaches, among others. Any of these could be women. The only seriously man-exclusive item on this list is the beard kit (and there are women with beards...).
              </p>
              <p>
               And besides that, half these gifts are lame. I can see that ping-pong kit being used once or twice and then forgotten about. A for concept, F for execution.
              </p>
